 inputah bhashaa It is said that there is no success and failure in science
 sirf prayog hota he
 And every experiment gets to learn something new
 taaki, aglaa prayog or behatar ho sake
 The Chandrayaan-2 moon mission of the Indian Space Agency ISRO (indian Space Research Organization - ISRO) has also proved to be a very learning experiment for ISRO scientists
 kai chijen pehali baar hui
 Many technologies were developed for the first time
 antariksh main kaksha badalane ke dauraan tay gati or tay duuri main zyada aage bade
 That is, better orbit maneuvering was done
 isse chandrayan-2 ke eendhan ko bachaane main madad mili
 
 aaie
 
 
 Know what the ISRO learned from this Chandrayaan-2 mission
 isro ne pehali baar banaaya lander or roverrus ne pehle chandrayan-2 ke liye lander dene kii baat kahi thi, lekin usne kuch samay baad manaa kar diya tha
 After this ISRO scientists decided that they would make their own lander
 apana rover banaaenge
 ISRO scientists also made both
 lander or rover ko banane ke liye khud hi research kiya
 Designed
 phir use banaaya
 All these took about 11 years
 ye sabhi swadeshi takanic se banaae gaye
 Rover was built and handed over to ISRO in 2015 by Hindustan Aeronautics Limited
 vahiin, vikram lander kii shuruaati dizin isro ke spes aplicoshan centre ahmedabad ne banaaya tha
 Later it was developed by the URSC of Bengaluru
 2
 It was not the first time that lander-rover was sent to a natural satellite
 Before that Chandrayaan-2 did not send lander or rover to any satellite
 ye pehali baar he ki isro ke vaigyanikon ne kisi prakritik upgrah par apana lander or rover bheja
 Even though Vikram Lander has not landed properly on the fixed route and fixed place, but he is on the moon
 agar sab sahi rahata to lander or rover abhi chand ke vaataavaran, jameen, rasinic gunvatttaon kii jaanch kar rahaa hota
 ISRO would have been getting beautiful pictures of the moon
 3
 India is the first country in the world and ISRO is the first space agency in the world to have launched its mission to the moon's south pole
 isse pehle aisa kisi bhi desh ne nahin kiya
 Even though the mission was not completely successful, Vikram Lander is still at the south pole of the moon
 isro vaigyanik lagaataar vikram lander se sampark sthapit karne main lage hai

 superkings ne raina (32 gend main 62 ran, chah chakke, chaar chauke) ke tabadatod ardhshtak kii madad se aath wicket par 181 ran banaae

 ishwar pandey ne bhi kifayati gendbaaji karte hue chaar over main 21 ran dekar ek wicket chatakaaya

 aaarasibi kii chaar maichon main yah teesri haar he or team antim paaydaan par chal rahi he

 kohli ne 42 gend kaa saamana karte hue chaar chauke or do chakke maare
 Nehra also got Harshal Patel (00) off the next ball to take his fourth wicket
 david visi ne 20 gend main 22 ran kii pari kheli lekin team ko lakshya ke kareeb nahin pahunchaa paae
 Earlier, apart from Raina, openers Smith and du Plessis (33 not out off 18 balls, four fours, one six) also played excellent innings to lead the team to a strong score
 superkings kii team ek samay 200 ran ke aas paas pahunchati najar aa rahi thi lekin ikbaal abdulla (36 ran par do wicket) or yujavendra chaahal (40 ran par teen wicket) aaarasibi ko vaapasi dilaane main safal rahe
 The Superkings were able to add 57 runs in the final seven overs
 mishael stark or herschel patel ne kifayati gendbaaji karte hue chaar-chaar over main kramash: 24 or 28 ran dekar ek-ek wicket chatakaaya
 Coming to bat after losing the toss, the Chennai team lost the wicket of Brandon mccullum (04) in the second over, who gave an easy catch to Rosoyu off the leg-spinner Chahal
 smith or raina ne iske baad pari ko sambhala
 Raina welcomed David Wise with a six, while in the next over of this fast bowler, Smith hit two sixes and a four off consecutive balls
 smith haalanki patel kii gend ko therdman par khilne kii koshish main wicketiper dinesh karthik ko kaich de baithe jisase raina ke saath unki 58 ran kii pari kaa ant hua
 Smith hit three sixes and as many fours in 29 balls
 tippaniyan Raina then added 54 runs in just four overs with captain Mahendra Singh Dhoni (13) increasing the run pace
 dhoni ne patel or visi par chauke maare jabaki raina ne abdulla kii gend ko long aan par chah ran ke liye bheja
 Raina hit a four in the 12th over of Abdullah and then hit a six to take the team's score beyond 100 runs
 raina ne agle over main chaahal par lagaataar teen chhakkon ke saath 31 gend main ardhashatak puraa kiya
 He, however, caught Rossoy at long off in an attempt to score another six off the next ball
 chaahal ne dhoni ko divilliars ke haathon kaich karake superkings ko chauthaa jhatka diya
 Abdullah gave a double blow to Chennai by getting Ravindra Jadeja (08) caught by Kohli and Dwayne Bravo (05) at the hands of de Villiers
 visi ne ravichandran aswin (05) ko pavilion bheja jabaki stark ne mohit sharma (02) ko bold kiya
 Dwayne Bravo then took a brilliant catch from Karthik off Pandey's ball and RCB scored 61 for three
 abi divilliars (14) ne aate hi ravindra jadeja or pandey par chakke jade
 However, he was run out due to misunderstanding with Kohli
 ipel main padaarpan kar rahe sabase yuva khilaadi 17 varshiya sarfaraj khan (11) ne jadeja par covers ke upar se chakka maaraa lekin baayen haath ke isi spinner kii gend par deep midwicket par mohit ko kaich de baithe
 Kohli hit two fours on Bravo while completing a 40-ball half-century with a six over Jadeja
 aaarasibi ko antim chaar over main jeet ke liye 59 ran kii jarurat thi or dwen smith ne nehra ke pari ke 17wein over kii pehali hi gend main boundry par kohli kaa shandaar kaich lapakkar mejabaan team kii rahi sahi ummid bhi tod di
 Kohli faced 42 balls and hit four fours and two sixes
 nehra ne agali gend par herschel patel (00) ko bhi pavilion bhejkar apana chauthaa wicket hasil kiya
 David Wise scored 22 runs in 20 balls but could not reach the team close to the target
 isse pehle raina ke alaava salaami ballebaaj smith or du plasis (18 gend main naabad 33, chaar chauke, ek chakka) ne bhi umdaa paariyaan khelkar team ko majboot score tak pahunchaaya
 The Superkings team seemed to be approaching 200 runs at one time but Iqbal Abdullah (2 wickets for 36 runs) and Yuzvendra Chahal (3 wickets for 40 runs) were able to get RCB back
 superkings antim saat over main 57 ran hi jod paae
 Mitchell Starc and Harshal Patel bowled economically, taking one wicket each for 24 and 28 runs in four overs
 tas harkar ballebaaji karne utari chennai kii team ne duusare over main hi brandan maikulam (04) kaa wicket ganvaa diya jinhone leg spinner chaahal kii gend par rosoyu ko aasaan kaich thamaya
 Smith and Raina then handled the innings
 raina ne david visi kaa swaagat chakke ke saath kiya jabaki is tej gendbaaj ke agle over main smith ne lagaataar gendon par do chakke or ek chaukaa maaraa
 Smith, however, was caught by wicketkeeper Dinesh Karthik in an attempt to play Patel's ball at third man, ending his 58-run knock with Raina
 smith ne 29 gend main teen chakke or itane hi chauke maare
 The comments raina ne iske baad captain mahendra singh dhoni (13) ke saath sirf chaar over main 54 ran jodakar ran gati main ijapha kiya
 Dhoni hit Patel and Yasey for fours while Raina sent Abdullah to long-on for a six
 raina ne abdulla ke pari ke 12wein over main chaukaa or phir chakka jadkar team kaa score 100 ran ke paar pahunchaaya
 Raina completed a 31-ball half-century with three consecutive sixes over Chahal in the next over
 vah haalanki agali gend par ek or chakka jadne kii koshish main long aaf par rosoyu ko kaich de baithe
 Chahal gave the fourth blow to the Superkings by getting Dhoni caught by de Villiers
 abdulla ne ravindra jadeja (08) ko kohli jabaki dwen braavo (05) ko divilliars ke haathon kaich karake chennai ko doharaa jhatka diya

 Immunity: The reason behind getting sick again and again is the weakening of our immunity
 rog pratirohak kshamta hamen kai bimariyon se bachaa ke rakhti he
 There are many small diseases that our body can deal with on its own
 rog pratirohak kshamta ke kamjor hone par bimariyon kaa asar jaldi hota he
 In such a situation, the body becomes weak and we begin to fall sick
 kuch bachche bahut jaldi-jaldi biimaar padate hai
 The reason for this is the weakening of their immunity
 kamjor immune system (weak Immune System) vaale bacchon ko mausam badalte hi sardi (cold), khaansee (cough), zukam, bukhaar (fever) jaisi samasyaayein honi shuru ho jaati hai
 Immunity provides protection from many types of bacterial infections, fungal infections
 in baton se yah to spasht ho jaataa he ki immune power ke kamjor hone par biimaar hone kii ashanka bad jaati he

 Joined as an assistant, and by which he not only earned immense wealth, but also established extensive political contacts
 agar lakshmikant or sudhir sharma par lage aaropon kii baat karen, to donon ne haath ai takat ke boote galat tareekon se athaah paisa kamaaya
 Both are alleged to have played a key role in the Vyapam scam, which had been confined to Madhya Pradesh for many years, but has become a national scandal in the last few days as there are discussions that more than 30 people involved in the scam are mysterious Have been killed by vyaapman ghotaale ke naam us sanstha ke naam vyavsaayik pariksha mandal (sankshep main vyaapman) se padaa, jo rajya ke collejon main daakhile ke saath-saath lagbhag 40 sarkari vibhaagon main bhartiyon ke liye bhi parikshaayen yojit karaati he
 Bribes were taken for writing examinations from someone else in place of real candidates, and this led to accusations of illegal earnings by big tutors and senior bureaucrats
 48-varshiya sudhir sharma ne rashtriya swayamsevak sangh dwaara sanchalit ek skool or baad main vidisha ke ek ejineering college main adhyaaapak ke rup main naukari kii
 Sudhir met Laxmikant Sharma in Vidisha, and Laxmikant was a legislator at that time
 varsh 2003 main lakshmikant sharma jab uma bharti kii sarkaar main khanan mantri ban gaye, sudhir ne unke staff ke rup main kaam karnaa shuru kiya, or varsh 2006 main sudhir ne khanan ke kshetra main bhagya aajamaane ke liye vah naukari bhi chhod di
 The move proved to be a 'gold mine' for Sudhir, and he then acquired VNS Group, a group of colleges that provided engineering and academic education

 In the holy month of Ramadan, people of Muslim society fast for 30 days
 is dauraan rojaa rakhane waalon ko is maheene main khan-paan par vishesh dhyaan dene kii salaah di jaati he
 Nothing is eaten or drunk during the day of fasting
 roje main iftaar or sahari ke bich ke samay main hi khan-paan kiya jaataa he
 It is recommended to drink as much water as iftar to sahari
 doctoron kaa kahana he ki roje ke dauraan neend puri na lene se aap biimaar bhi ho sakate hai
 At the time of Roja, Dr
 Khan advises to pay special attention to things of drink
 is dauraan gairajaruri chizon ko khaane se bachanaa chahie
 Do with fried things It is advisable to avoid eating fried things during fasting
 sahari ke samay anda, aate kii roti yaa parantha, taaje fal aadi khaane se sehat thik rahati he
 Keep in mind that you should not drink too much coffee or soda at the time of sahari saath hi sahari main biryani, kebab, pizza, or fast foods nahin khaane chahie
 They can affect your health
 roje main iftaar ke dauraan khajur khaanaa chahie
 Dates are beneficial for health
 khajur main aayran hota he, jisase sharir ko urja milti he
 Fried food is harmful to the body during Iftar
 iftaar main tala hua khaanaa khaane se bachanaa chahie
 Eat fiber-rich things - If you have indigestion problem during Ramadan, you should eat fiber-rich things to digest it
 iftaar ke samay khaane khate samay kam se kam pani pinaa chahie
 Because drinking much water does not digest food
 jo sharir ke liye hanikaarak ho saktaa he
 More and more protein should be eaten in the month of Ramadan
 adhik maatra main protein khaane se kam bhukh lagati he
 Sick people should not eat it - Those who have heart disease and diabetes disease should avoid eating kebabs, biryani and chicken
 iftaar se lekar sehari tak khaanaa khaane ke samay haath achche se dho lene chahie kyonki bhukh rahane par sharir main kamajori aa jaati he or keetanu jaldi hamalaa karte hai
 Do not go out in the sun at all, on a daily-summer day there is an increased risk of dehydration
 aise main rojedaar dhoop main baahar na nikalen
 If there is blood pressure or sugar, they should not keep fasting because sugar can be uncontrolled in that case
 agar kisi paristhiti main baahar nikalne kii naubat aae to tauliya yaa gamchaa baandhakar nikle

 The train accident on Sunday near Kanpur in Uttar Pradesh is considered one of the worst rail accidents in the country so far
 is haadase main maare gaye logon kaa aankada 142 tak pahunch gaya he

 kanpur ke paas pukhraayaan main hue rail haadase ke baad bhi jaanch ke aadesh de die gaye hai jaisaa ki abhi tak har haadason ke baad hota aayaa he
 Initial investigations indicated that the accident may have occurred due to a railway track malfunction
 driver kii report se laaparvaahee kii baat saamne ai he
 By the way, many small and big train accidents happen every year in our country and 86 percent of these accidents are due to human mistakes
 lekin is tathy se inkaar nahin kiya ja saktaa he ki america or china ke baad duniya main teesraa sabase bada rail system hone ke baavjood bhartiya rail ab bhi british kaal ke infrastakchar par chal rahi he
 According to which the railway traffic pressure is increasing on the tracks, the infrastructure is not being upgraded accordingly
 ek ore to sarkaar bullate train chalaane kii yojana bana rahi he, duusari ore moolbhoot dhaanche main badlaav nahin hone kii vajah se saamaanya trainon ko haadason se bachaane main sarkaar naakaam dikh rahi he
 Safety is a major issue in front of the railway
 signling system main chook or anti coligen divises kii kami se bhi aae din haadase hote rahete hai
 1
 infrastakchar kii kamike chalate rail haadase kii yah koi nai ghatana nahin he
 About 35 years ago, a severe railway accident took place in Bihar in which about 800 people were killed
 6 june 1981 ko ek paisanger train maanasi or saharsa ke bich patari se utar gai or baagmati nadi main dub gai
 There were about 800 passengers in this train
 ghatana ke 5 din baad kareeb 200 shavon ko nadi se nikaala gaya lekin baaki musafiron kii laashen tak nahin mil pain thi
 It is said that their dead bodies may have been swept away by the strong current of the river
 kaha gaya ki baadh kaa pani patariyon tak pahunch gaya tha is vajah se train haadase kaa shikaar ho gai
 That is, even 35 years ago, the railway infrastructure was like that in many places
 2
 a similar accident occurred in Kerala seven years after the Saharsa railway accident
 bangalore se trivendrum ja rahi island express 8 july, 1988 ko kerala main ashtamudi lake main gir gai, jisamen 107 log maare gaye the
 The accident took place on the Peruman Bridge in Kollam district when 9 coaches of the train derailed
 inamen se do dibbe nadi main gir gaye the
 The real cause of this accident is not yet known
 kisi ne kaha ki railway trek or train ke pahiyon main gadabadi kii vajah se haadasa hua to kisi ne bataaya ki railway brij par mentenance kaa kaam chal rahaa tha or train dhimi raftaar ke bajaay teji se brij ko paar kar rahi thi
 In such a situation, 28 years ago, the condition of the tracks and the wheels of the rail was the same as it is today
 3
 On 20 August 1995, a severe railway accident occurred near Firozabad on the delhi-kanpur section in Uttar Pradesh
 us vakt kanpur se dilli ja rahi kalindi express ne trek par ai ek gaay ko takkar maar di thi
 After this collision there was some technical fault in the train and the driver stopped the train
 isi bich usee trek par peeche se aa rahi purushottam express ne kalindi express ko joardaar takkar maar di
 400 people were killed and around 300 were injured in this accident
 is haadase ko bharat main hui rail durghatnaon main sabase bhayaavah haadason main gina jaataa he
 Today, while a 400-500 km speed bullet train is being planned in India, animals are common on the tracks here
 agar train kii patariyon ko contile taron se gher diya jaae to aise haadase roke ja sakate hai
 4
 9 sitambar 2002 ko haavda-dilli rajdhani express bihar ke aurangabad main haadase kaa shikaar ho gai thi
 The accident happened when the train was passing through a river bridge
 train ke 14 dibbe patari se utre or nadi main gir gaye
 100 people were killed and 150 were injured in this accident
 haadase kii vajah is pul par patariyon kaa kamjor hona bataaya gaya
 This railway bridge over the river was built in the year 1916
 jaankaar kehete hai ki 1930 se pehle bane desh ke zyadatar railway pul khatarnaak hai
 High speed trains passing through these bridges are not free from danger
 5
 The list of accidents due to dilapidated tracks on bridges is quite large
 14 sitambar 1997 ko madhya pradesh ke bilaspur jile main ahmedabad-haavda express ek nadi main giri jisamen 81 log maare gaye the
 On the night of 4 August 2015, the Kamayani Express going from Mumbai to Varanasi and mumbai-jabalpur Janata Express derailed near Kudwa railway station in Harda district of Madhya Pradesh
 is haadase main kam se 25 log maare gaye the
 It was said that due to heavy rains, the soil under the tracks had sunk, causing this accident
 is rail haadase ke baad bhi ek baar phir infrastakchar kii kami kii baat saamne ai
 6
 punjab ke khanna main 26 november 1998 ko hue bheeshan rail haadase main kam se kam 212 log maare gaye the
 The accident occurred when the Jammuutti Sealdah Express crashed into the frontier mail compartments
 in donon trainon main kul milakar kareeb 2000 log savaar the
 The Frontier Mail (golden Temple Mail) going from Ludhiana to Ambala derailed between Khanna and Chavapail stations
 is vajah se is train ke kuch dibbe bagal vaale trek par ja gire
 At the same time, the Jammuutvi coming from the other direction collided with the coaches that fell on the Sealdah Express tracks
 nahin liya sabakin haadason ke baad bhi bhartiya rail apane musafiron kii suraksha ko lekar kitni gambhir he, yah kanpur rail haadase se saaf ho gaya he
 The Justice HR Khanna Committee, formed in 1998, made various recommendations regarding safety
 ye siforishein railway ne maan to lee hai lekin ye abhi kaagajon par hi dikhti hai, jamini taur par inhen lagu kiya janaa baaki he
